***передвигать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:передвигать.html>передви́гать</a> (12284)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">передви́г-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">peredvíg-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передвигать.html>передвига́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">peredvigátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передвинуть.html>передви́нуть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to move, to shift
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:передвигать.html>передвига́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:стрелок.html>стре́лку</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>часо́в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вперед.html>вперёд</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:назад.html>наза́д</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>peredvigátʹ</b> strélku časóv vperjód (nazád)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to put the hands of a clock forward/on (back); put a clock forward/on (back)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:медленно.html>ме́дленно</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:передвигать.html>передвига́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>но́ги</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">médlenno <b>peredvigája</b> nógi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">slowly dragging one's feet</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:еле.html>е́ле</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>но́ги</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:передвигать.html>передвига́ть</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jéle nógi <b>peredvigátʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be barely able to drag oneself along [to put one foot in front of the other]</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(time)</i> to shift, to move
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:передвигать.html>передвига́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:срок.html>сро́ки</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:исполнение.html>исполне́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>peredvigátʹ</b> sróki ispolnénija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to change the deadline (for)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:передвигать.html>передвига́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:более.html>бо́лее</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:поздний.html>по́зднюю</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дата.html>да́ту</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>peredvigátʹ</b> na bóleje pózdnjuju dátu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to carry over; put off</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:передвигать.html>передвига́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:более.html>бо́лее</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ранний.html>ра́ннюю</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дата.html>да́ту</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>peredvigátʹ</b> na bóleje ránnjuju dátu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to bring/set forward; put ahead</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <i>(to the other position)</i> to move, to transfer</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передвижение.html>передвиже́ние</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">peredvižénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">передви́жник</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">peredvížnik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передвижной.html>передвижно́й</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">peredvižnój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:двигать.html>дви́гать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dvígatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передвигать.html>передви́гать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">peredvígatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to move (everything or many things)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всю</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мебель.html>ме́бель</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:передвигать.html>передви́гать</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vsju mébelʹ <b>peredvígatʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to move all the furniture</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:передвинуть.html>передви́нуть</a> (14058)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:двинуть.html>дви́нуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dvínutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передвинуть.html>передви́нуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">peredvínutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передвигать.html>передвига́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to move, to shift
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стол.html>стол</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:надо.html>на́до</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:передвинуть.html>передви́нуть</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">stol nádo <b>peredvínutʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the table should be moved</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:передвинуть.html>передви́нуть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:стрелок.html>стре́лку</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>часо́в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вперед.html>вперёд</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:назад.html>наза́д</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>peredvínutʹ</b> strélku časóv vperjód (nazád)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to put the hands of a clock forward/on (back); put a clock forward/on (back)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(time)</i> to shift, to move
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:передвинуть.html>передви́нуть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:срок.html>сро́ки</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:исполнение.html>исполне́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>peredvínutʹ</b> sróki ispolnénija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to change the deadline (for)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:передвинуть.html>передви́нуть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:более.html>бо́лее</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:поздний.html>по́зднюю</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дата.html>да́ту</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>peredvínutʹ</b> na bóleje pózdnjuju dátu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to carry over; put off</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:передвинуть.html>передви́нуть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:более.html>бо́лее</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ранний.html>ра́ннюю</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дата.html>да́ту</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>peredvínutʹ</b> na bóleje ránnjuju dátu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to bring/set forward; put ahead</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <i>(to the other position)</i> to move, to transfer</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передвижение.html>передвиже́ние</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">peredvižénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">передви́жник</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">peredvížnik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передвижной.html>передвижно́й</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">peredvižnój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***передел.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:передел.html>переде́л</a> (18332)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Deverbal of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">передели́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">peredelítʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to repartition, to redivide, to redistribute</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передел.html>переде́л</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">peredél</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передел.html>переде́ла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передел.html>переде́лы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передел.html>переде́лов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>repartition, redivision, redistribution
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:передел.html>переде́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мир.html>ми́ра</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>peredél</b> míra</i> ― <span class="e-translation">redivision of the world</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:передел.html>переде́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:земля.html>земли</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>peredél</b> zemli</i> ― <span class="e-translation">re-allotment of land</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Deverbal of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переделать.html>переде́лать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">peredélatʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to redo</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передел.html>переде́л</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">peredél</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передел.html>переде́ла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передел.html>переде́лы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передел.html>переде́лов</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">переде́льный</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">metallurgy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> reprocessing or remelting of lower-grade metal into higher-grade metal</li>

***переделать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:переделать.html>переде́лать</a> (8548)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:делать.html>де́лать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">délatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переделать.html>переде́лать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">peredélatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переделывать.html>переде́лывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to make over, to alter <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to change the form or structure of</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to do anew, to rework</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:переделка.html>переде́лка</a> (14933)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переделать.html>переде́лать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">peredélatʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to alter, to redo</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переделка.html>переде́лка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">peredélka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переделка.html>переде́лки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переделка.html>переде́лки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переделка.html>переде́лок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>alteration, redo
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отдать.html>отда́ть</a> что́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:переделка.html>переде́лку</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">otdátʹ štó-libo v <b>peredélku</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">have smth altered</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:переделка.html>переде́лка</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:старый.html>ста́рого</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сюжет.html>сюже́та</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>peredélka</b> stárovo sjužéta</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">remake</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> trouble, mess, fix, scrape
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:попасть.html>попа́сть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:переделка.html>переде́лку</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">popástʹ v <b>peredélku</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">get into a mess/fix/scrape, run into trouble</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бывать.html>быва́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:разный.html>ра́зных</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:переделка.html>переде́лках</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">byvál ja v ráznyx <b>peredélkax</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I've been in a tight corner many a time</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***передо.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:передо.html>передо</a> (3269)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Preposition">Preposition</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передо.html>пе́редо</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">péredo</span>) <i>+ instrumental case</i> (see <b><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перед.html>пе́ред</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">péred</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>in front of, before</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:передо.html>Передо</a></b> is used instead of <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перед.html>пе́ред</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">péred</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> before <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мной</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">mnoj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мно́ю</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">mnóju</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and nouns in the instrumental case that start with <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ль.html>ль</a></b>, <b>л</b>, <b>м</b>, <b>р</b> + consonant.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***передовик.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:передовик.html>передови́к</a> (22665)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передовик.html>передови́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">peredovík</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передовик.html>передовика́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передовик.html>передовики́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передовик.html>передовико́в</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">передови́чка</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chiefly Soviet Union</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> pacemaker, model worker (especially winning distinctions)</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перед.html>пе́ред</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">péred</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ово́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дозировка.html>дозиро́вка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">doziróvka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; probably a calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">overdose</i> or  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Überdosis</i>.

***передохнуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:передохнуть.html>передохну́ть</a> (8583)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передохнуть.html>передохну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">peredoxnútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">передыха́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to take a break, to have a break, to have a rest, to take a breath <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to have a short rest period in one's work</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:передохнуть.html>передохни́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:перед.html>пе́ред</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дальний.html>да́льней</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дорога.html>доро́гой</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Peredoxní</b> péred dálʹnej dorógoj.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>Take a break</b> before a long journey.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передохнуть.html>передо́хнуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">peredóxnutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">передыха́ть</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дохнуть.html>до́хнуть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to die off, to extinct, to die in masses <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">especially of animals or when likening people with animals</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>Мы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>все</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:здесь.html>здесь</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:передохнуть.html>передо́хнем</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:без.html>без</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>тебя́</a>!</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">My vse zdesʹ <b>peredóxnem</b> bez tebjá!</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">We're all gonna die here without you!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:передряга.html>передря́га</a> (23911)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">передра́ть(ся)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">peredrátʹ(sja)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́га</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-jága</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передряга.html>передря́га</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">peredrjága</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передряга.html>передря́ги</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передряга.html>передря́ги</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передряга.html>передря́г</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> scrape, fight
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:попасть.html>попа́сть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:передряга.html>передря́гу</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">popástʹ v <b>peredrjágu</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to get into a scrape</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> trouble, mess</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:передумать.html>переду́мавший</a> (6332)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передумать.html>переду́мавший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">peredúmavšij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past active perfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передумать.html>переду́мать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">peredúmatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<table style="float:right; clear:right; margin-left:0.5em; margin-bottom:0.5em; border: 1px solid 6699CC; border-collapse:collapse;" cellpadding="2" rules="all" width="210" class="morfotable ru">
<tbody><tr>

***передумать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:передумать.html>переду́мать</a> (6332)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:думать.html>ду́мать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dúmatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передумать.html>переду́мать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">peredúmatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">переду́мывать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to change one's mind</li>
<li>to think over multiple things or many times</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передышка.html>переды́шка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">peredýška</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передышка.html>переды́шки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передышка.html>переды́шки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передышка.html>переды́шек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>respite, breathing space
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:давать.html>дава́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:передышка.html>переды́шку</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">davátʹ <b>peredýšku</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">grant/give a respite</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:давать.html>дава́я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:минута.html>мину́ты</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:передышка.html>переды́шки</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne davája ni minúty <b>peredýški</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">without a moment's respite</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
